<script type="module"> /** * canonical() — Same implementation as unified-test.html * MUST be byte-for-byte identical for hash verification to work. */ function canonical(obj) { return _canonicalize(obj); } function _canonicalize(obj) { if (obj === null) return 'null'; if (typeof obj === 'boolean') return obj ? 'true' : 'false'; if (typeof obj === 'number') return _canonicalNumber(obj); if (typeof obj === 'string') return JSON.stringify(obj); if (Array.isArray(obj)) { return '[' + obj.map(_canonicalize).join(',') + ']'; } if (typeof obj === 'object') { const keys = Object.keys(obj).sort(); const pairs = keys.map(k => JSON.stringify(k) + ':' + _canonicalize(obj[k])); return '{' + pairs.join(',') + '}'; } throw new TypeError(`JCS: unsupported type ${typeof obj}`); } function _canonicalNumber(n) { if (!Number.isFinite(n)) { throw new Error('JCS: NaN and Infinity are not permitted'); } if (Number.isInteger(n)) return String(n); let s = n.toFixed(20); s = s.replace(/0+$/, '').replace(/\.$/, ''); if (s.includes('e') || s.includes('E')) { s = _expandScientific(s); } return s; } function _expandScientific(s) { const [mantissa, expStr] = s.toLowerCase().split('e'); const exp = parseInt(expStr, 10); let digits = mantissa.replace('.', ''); if (exp >= 0) { if (exp >= digits.length - 1) { return digits + '0'.repeat(exp - digits.length + 1); } return digits.slice(0, exp + 1) + '.' + digits.slice(exp + 1).replace(/0+$/, '').replace(/\.$/, ''); } else { return '0.' + '0'.repeat(-exp - 1) + digits; } } async function canonicalHash(obj) { const bytes = new TextEncoder().encode(canonical(obj)); const hashBuffer = await crypto.subtle.digest('SHA-256', bytes); return Array.from(new Uint8Array(hashBuffer)) .map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0')) .join(''); } /** * Verify Ed25519 signature using tweetnacl */ async function verifySignature(messageBytes, signatureHex, publicKeyHex) { const nacl = window.nacl || await loadTweetNacl(); const signature = hexToBytes(signatureHex); const publicKey = hexToBytes(publicKeyHex); return nacl.sign.detached.verify(messageBytes, signature, publicKey); } async function loadTweetNacl() { if (typeof window !== 'undefined' && window.nacl) return window.nacl; // Load from CDN return new Promise((resolve, reject) => { const script = document.createElement('script'); script.src = 'https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/tweetnacl@1.0.3/nacl-fast.min.js'; script.onload = () => resolve(window.nacl); script.onerror = reject; document.head.appendChild(script); }); } function hexToBytes(hex) { const bytes = new Uint8Array(hex.length / 2); for (let i = 0; i < hex.length; i += 2) { bytes[i / 2] = parseInt(hex.slice(i, i + 2), 16); } return bytes; } // Main verification window.verifyArtifact = async function() { const input = document.getElementById('artifactInput').value.trim(); const errorEl = document.getElementById('errorMsg'); const resultsEl = document.getElementById('results'); errorEl.classList.remove('active'); resultsEl.classList.remove('active'); try { const artifact = JSON.parse(input); // Validate structure if (!artifact.version || !artifact.timestamp || !artifact.identity || !artifact.answers) { throw new Error('Missing required fields in artifact'); } // Recompute hash const payload = { version: artifact.version, timestamp: artifact.timestamp, identity: artifact.identity, answers: artifact.answers, }; const recomputedHash = await canonicalHash(payload); const hashValid = recomputedHash === artifact.hash; // Verify signature (requires public key — in practice, this would be resolved // from identity fingerprint via a registry or the artifact would include pubkey) let sigValid = false; let sigChecked = false; if (artifact.signature && artifact.publicKey) { const messageBytes = new TextEncoder().encode(canonical(payload)); sigValid = await verifySignature(messageBytes, artifact.signature, artifact.publicKey); sigChecked = true; } // Update UI updateStatusCard('hash', hashValid); updateStatusCard('sig', sigValid, !sigChecked); document.getElementById('detailVersion').textContent = artifact.version; document.getElementById('detailTimestamp').textContent = artifact.timestamp; document.getElementById('detailIdentity').textContent = artifact.identity; document.getElementById('detailAnswers').textContent = `Decision: ${artifact.answers.decision}, Uncertainty: ${artifact.answers.uncertainty}, Change: ${artifact.answers.change}`; document.getElementById('detailAlgo').textContent = artifact.algorithm || 'Unknown'; document.getElementById('detailHash').textContent = artifact.hash; document.getElementById('detailSig').textContent = artifact.signature ? (artifact.signature.slice(0, 48) + '...') : 'Not provided'; resultsEl.classList.add('active'); } catch (e) { errorEl.textContent = 'Error: ' + e.message; errorEl.classList.add('active'); } }; function updateStatusCard(type, valid, unchecked = false) { const card = document.getElementById(type + 'Card'); const icon = document.getElementById(type + 'Icon'); const value = document.getElementById(type + 'Value'); card.className = 'status-card ' + (valid ? 'valid' : 'invalid'); if (unchecked) { icon.textContent = '?'; value.textContent = 'No Key'; card.className = 'status-card'; return; } if (valid) { icon.textContent = '✓'; value.textContent = 'Valid'; } else { icon.textContent = '✗'; value.textContent = 'Invalid'; } } </script> '''

@mohammadyounus128198-cyber

Great drop — the flow, JCS canonicalization, and artifact wiring all look solid. To make the signing path fully deterministic and browser-proof, here are two minimal fixes you should apply.

Why this matters

WebCrypto Ed25519 private keys typically import as PKCS#8, not raw; your current importKey('raw', ...) will often fail.
The dynamic import of tweetnacl from a CDN won’t work because that file isn’t an ES module.
Result: on many browsers the fallback never kicks in and signing fails silently.
Minimal diffs

Ensure NaCl is loaded as a global before the module script
Add this right before your <script type="module"> block:
<script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/tweetnacl@1.0.3/nacl.min.js" crossorigin="anonymous"></script>
Always sign with NaCl (simple, deterministic, cross‑browser)
Replace your current signPayload() with the following. It signs canonical(payload) using the 64‑byte NaCl secretKey (identity.privateKey should be that secretKey).
async function signPayload(payload, secretKey) {
  const bytes = new TextEncoder().encode(canonical(payload));
  // secretKey must be a 64-byte Uint8Array (nacl.sign.keyPair().secretKey)
  const sig = nacl.sign.detached(bytes, secretKey);
  return Array.from(sig).map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0')).join('');
}
Avoid the window.event implicit global in copyArtifact
Change the onclick and function signature so it’s portable:
In HTML:
<button class="btn-copy" onclick="copyArtifact(this)">📋 Copy Artifact</button>
In script:
window.copyArtifact = function (btnEl) {
  navigator.clipboard.writeText(canonical(artifact));
  btnEl.textContent = '✓ Copied';
  setTimeout(() => (btnEl.textContent = '📋 Copy Artifact'), 2000);
};
Strongly recommended alignment in identity.js
To keep the whole flow deterministic and consistent with the UI:

Generate and persist the keypair with tweetnacl:
const { publicKey, secretKey } = nacl.sign.keyPair()
Store secretKey (64 bytes) and publicKey (32 bytes) in IndexedDB.
Compute fingerprint = SHA‑256(publicKey) hex (you can keep showing the truncated form in UI).
That gives you:

One canonical signer everywhere (NaCl), zero WebCrypto private‑key format variance.
WebCrypto still used for SHA‑256 (fine and widely supported).
Optional niceties (later)

Add signature verification to the external verifier by including publicKey in the artifact or by resolving it from a local registry keyed by fingerprint.
If you want to bind this artifact into your Merkle seal (per your v2.0 system), record artifact.hash in the manifest and let CI verify it — no code changes needed here.
Want me to open a follow-up PR that applies the three diffs above to unified-test.html and refactors identity.js to NaCl-only keypairs? If yes, say “plan code changes” and I’ll enumerate the exact edits.

@mohammadyounus128198-cyber

Great progress — the verifier UI and hash check are solid. Two surgical tweaks will get you full signature verification and eliminate future drift.

What to fix

Embed the public key in the artifact
Your verifier only verifies the signature if artifact.publicKey exists. The generator (unified-test.html) doesn’t add it yet.
Make signing deterministic across key backends
If identity.privateKey is 32 bytes (WebCrypto export), use WebCrypto to sign.
If it’s 64 bytes (tweetnacl secretKey), use NaCl.
Avoid dynamic CDN imports inside sign; rely on window.nacl if you already include it.
De-drift canonicalization
Prefer importing the same canonical.js in verify.html instead of inlining the JCS logic.
Minimal code changes

A) unified-test.html (module script): add hex helper, include publicKey, harden signPayload

// Add once near top of module script
const toHex = (u8) => Array.from(u8).map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2,'0')).join('');

// Replace your signPayload with this version
async function signPayload(payload, privKeyU8) {
  const msg = new TextEncoder().encode(canonical(payload));

  // Case 1: WebCrypto Ed25519 (32‑byte raw private key)
  if (crypto.subtle && privKeyU8.byteLength === 32) {
    const key = await crypto.subtle.importKey('raw', privKeyU8, { name: 'Ed25519' }, false, ['sign']);
    const sig = await crypto.subtle.sign('Ed25519', key, msg);
    return toHex(new Uint8Array(sig));
  }

  // Case 2: tweetnacl (64‑byte secretKey)
  if (typeof window !== 'undefined' && window.nacl && privKeyU8.byteLength === 64) {
    const sig = window.nacl.sign.detached(msg, privKeyU8);
    return toHex(sig);
  }

  throw new Error('No compatible Ed25519 signer found. Ensure identity.js yields 32B WebCrypto key or 64B NaCl secretKey.');
}

// In sealArtifact(), add publicKey to artifact
artifact = {
  ...payload,
  hash,
  signature: sig,
  publicKey: toHex(identity.publicKey),   // ← add this line
  algorithm: 'Ed25519-SHA256',
};
B) verify.html: use the shared canonical.js (recommended)

Replace the inline canonical() with an import, and keep your current inline as a small fallback if import fails.
<script type="module">
let canonical, canonicalHash;

try {
  // Primary: import the exact same module the generator uses
  const mod = await import('./canonical.js');
  canonical = mod.canonical;
  canonicalHash = mod.canonicalHash;
} catch (_) {
  // Fallback: tiny local version (keep your current inline copy here)
  // ... your existing canonical(), _canonicalize(), _canonicalNumber(), canonicalHash() ...
}
</script>
Quick test checklist

Generate: Open unified-test.html, complete the quiz, copy the artifact JSON.
Verify: Paste into verify.html. Expect:
Hash Validity: Valid
Signature Validity: Valid
Tamper test: Change one character in answers.decision and re-verify → Hash Invalid and Signature Invalid.
Seal/CI alignment

To mesh with your sealed-CI workflow (byte-level Merkle + domain-separated hashing), emit the artifact’s canonical hash as a leaf in your seal manifest and fail CI on any mismatch. This keeps the verifier UI, artifact generator, and CI root hash in lockstep.
If you want, I can prep a tiny PR plan to:

add publicKey to the artifact emitter,
refactor verify.html to import canonical.js,
and add a seal step that registers the artifact hash as a leaf.
Say “plan code changes” and I’ll outline the exact edits and paths.

PHASE 2: WEB-BASED STOCK TRADING SIMULATOR

File 1: marketData.ts — Data Adapter Layer
market_data_ts = '''/**

marketData.ts — Data Adapter Layer for Trading Simulator
Provides unified market data combining real analyst ratings
with realistic price simulation for backtesting and paper trading.
*/
export interface Stock {
symbol: string;
name: string;
sector: string;
}

export interface Quote {
symbol: string;
price: number; // Current price in cents (integer)
change: number; // Change from previous close in cents
changePercent: number;
volume: number;
timestamp: string; // ISO 8601
}

export interface AnalystRating {
symbol: string;
firm: string;
rating: 'buy' | 'hold' | 'sell' | 'strong_buy' | 'strong_sell';
targetPrice: number; // In cents
date: string; // ISO 8601
}

export interface MarketDataProvider {
getQuotes(symbols: string[]): Promise<Quote[]>;
getRatings(symbol: string): Promise<AnalystRating[]>;
getAvailableSymbols(): string[];
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// CSV Market Data Provider — Parses aapl_analyst_ratings.csv
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

export class CSVMarketDataProvider implements MarketDataProvider {
private ratings: Map<string, AnalystRating[]> = new Map();
private symbols: string[] = [];

constructor(csvContent: string) {
this.parseCSV(csvContent);
}

private parseCSV(content: string) {
const lines = content.trim().split('\n');
const headers = lines[0].split(',').map(h => h.trim().toLowerCase());

const symbolIdx = headers.indexOf('symbol');
const firmIdx = headers.indexOf('firm');
const ratingIdx = headers.indexOf('rating');
const targetIdx = headers.indexOf('target_price');
const dateIdx = headers.indexOf('date');

for (let i = 1; i < lines.length; i++) {
  const cols = this.parseLine(lines[i]);
  if (cols.length < headers.length) continue;

  const symbol = cols[symbolIdx]?.trim().toUpperCase();
  if (!symbol) continue;

  const rating: AnalystRating = {
    symbol,
    firm: cols[firmIdx]?.trim() || 'Unknown',
    rating: this.normalizeRating(cols[ratingIdx]?.trim() || 'hold'),
    targetPrice: Math.round(parseFloat(cols[targetIdx] || '0') * 100),
    date: cols[dateIdx]?.trim() || new Date().toISOString(),
  };

  if (!this.ratings.has(symbol)) {
    this.ratings.set(symbol, []);
    this.symbols.push(symbol);
  }
  this.ratings.get(symbol)!.push(rating);
}
}

private parseLine(line: string): string[] {
const result: string[] = [];
let current = '';
let inQuotes = false;

for (const char of line) {
  if (char === '"') {
    inQuotes = !inQuotes;
  } else if (char === ',' && !inQuotes) {
    result.push(current.trim());
    current = '';
  } else {
    current += char;
  }
}
result.push(current.trim());
return result;
}

private normalizeRating(r: string): AnalystRating['rating'] {
const map: Record<string, AnalystRating['rating']> = {
'buy': 'buy', 'b': 'buy',
'hold': 'hold', 'h': 'hold', 'neutral': 'hold',
'sell': 'sell', 's': 'sell',
'strong buy': 'strong_buy', 'strong_buy': 'strong_buy', 'sb': 'strong_buy',
'strong sell': 'strong_sell', 'strong_sell': 'strong_sell', 'ss': 'strong_sell',
};
return map[r.toLowerCase()] || 'hold';
}

async getQuotes(symbols: string[]): Promise<Quote[]> {
// In a real implementation, this would fetch from an API
// For simulation, we generate realistic quotes based on analyst targets
return symbols.map(sym => {
const ratings = this.ratings.get(sym) || [];
const avgTarget = ratings.length > 0
? ratings.reduce((s, r) => s + r.targetPrice, 0) / ratings.length
: 15000; // Default $150.00

  // Simulate current price near target with some variance
  const variance = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.1; // ±5%
  const price = Math.round(avgTarget * (1 + variance));
  
  return {
    symbol: sym,
    price,
    change: Math.round(price * (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.02),
    changePercent: parseFloat((Math.random() * 4 - 2).toFixed(2)),
    volume: Math.floor(Math.random() * 10000000) + 1000000,
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
  };
});
}

async getRatings(symbol: string): Promise<AnalystRating[]> {
return this.ratings.get(symbol.toUpperCase()) || [];
}

getAvailableSymbols(): string[] {
return [...this.symbols];
}
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Mock Price Generator — Realistic simulation for paper trading
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

export interface PriceModel {
drift: number; // Annualized expected return (decimal)
volatility: number; // Annualized volatility (decimal)
jumpProb: number; // Probability of jump per day
jumpSize: number; // Average jump size (decimal)
}

export class MockPriceGenerator implements MarketDataProvider {
private prices: Map<string, number> = new Map();
private models: Map<string, PriceModel> = new Map();
private lastUpdate: Map<string, number> = new Map();

constructor(initialPrices: Record<string, number>) {
Object.entries(initialPrices).forEach(([sym, price]) => {
this.prices.set(sym, Math.round(price * 100));
this.models.set(sym, {
drift: 0.08, // 8% annual return
volatility: 0.25, // 25% annual volatility
jumpProb: 0.02, // 2% daily jump probability
jumpSize: 0.05, // 5% average jump
});
this.lastUpdate.set(sym, Date.now());
});
}

async getQuotes(symbols: string[]): Promise<Quote[]> {
return symbols.map(sym => {
const currentPrice = this.prices.get(sym) || 10000;
const model = this.models.get(sym)!;
const lastTime = this.lastUpdate.get(sym) || Date.now();

  // Time since last update in trading days (approx)
  const daysElapsed = (Date.now() - lastTime) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24);
  
  // Geometric Brownian Motion step
  const dt = daysElapsed / 252; // Trading days per year
  const randomShock = this.gaussianRandom() * Math.sqrt(dt);
  const driftTerm = (model.drift - 0.5 * model.volatility ** 2) * dt;
  const volTerm = model.volatility * randomShock;
  
  let newPrice = currentPrice * Math.exp(driftTerm + volTerm);
  
  // Jump diffusion
  if (Math.random() < model.jumpProb * daysElapsed) {
    const jumpDir = Math.random() > 0.5 ? 1 : -1;
    newPrice *= (1 + jumpDir * model.jumpSize * Math.random());
  }
  
  newPrice = Math.max(1, Math.round(newPrice));
  const change = newPrice - currentPrice;
  
  this.prices.set(sym, newPrice);
  this.lastUpdate.set(sym, Date.now());
  
  return {
    symbol: sym,
    price: newPrice,
    change,
    changePercent: parseFloat(((change / currentPrice) * 100).toFixed(2)),
    volume: Math.floor(Math.random() * 10000000) + 1000000,
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
  };
});
}

async getRatings(symbol: string): Promise<AnalystRating[]> {
// Mock ratings for simulation
return [{
symbol: symbol.toUpperCase(),
firm: 'Mock Analytics',
rating: Math.random() > 0.5 ? 'buy' : 'hold',
targetPrice: Math.round((this.prices.get(symbol) || 10000) * (1 + (Math.random() - 0.3) * 0.2)),
date: new Date().toISOString(),
}];
}

getAvailableSymbols(): string[] {
return Array.from(this.prices.keys());
}

private gaussianRandom(): number {
// Box-Muller transform
const u1 = Math.random();
const u2 = Math.random();
return Math.sqrt(-2 * Math.log(u1)) * Math.cos(2 * Math.PI * u2);
}

setModel(symbol: string, model: PriceModel) {
this.models.set(symbol.toUpperCase(), model);
}
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Unified Market Data — Combines real ratings with simulated prices
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

export class UnifiedMarketData implements MarketDataProvider {
private csvProvider: CSVMarketDataProvider;
private mockGenerator: MockPriceGenerator;

constructor(csvContent: string, initialPrices: Record<string, number>) {
this.csvProvider = new CSVMarketDataProvider(csvContent);
this.mockGenerator = new MockPriceGenerator(initialPrices);
}

async getQuotes(symbols: string[]): Promise<Quote[]> {
// Use mock generator for prices, but enrich with analyst sentiment
const quotes = await this.mockGenerator.getQuotes(symbols);

return Promise.all(quotes.map(async q => {
  const ratings = await this.csvProvider.getRatings(q.symbol);
  if (ratings.length > 0) {
    // Adjust price slightly based on analyst consensus
    const buyCount = ratings.filter(r => r.rating.includes('buy')).length;
    const sellCount = ratings.filter(r => r.rating.includes('sell')).length;
    const sentiment = (buyCount - sellCount) / ratings.length;
    
    // Sentiment affects price by up to 2%
    const adjustment = 1 + sentiment * 0.02;
    q.price = Math.round(q.price * adjustment);
  }
  return q;
}));
}

async getRatings(symbol: string): Promise<AnalystRating[]> {
// Prefer real ratings, fall back to mock
const real = await this.csvProvider.getRatings(symbol);
return real.length > 0 ? real : this.mockGenerator.getRatings(symbol);
}

getAvailableSymbols(): string[] {
const real = this.csvProvider.getAvailableSymbols();
const mock = this.mockGenerator.getAvailableSymbols();
return [...new Set([...real, ...mock])];
}
}

// Factory function
export function getMarketData(
csvContent?: string,
initialPrices?: Record<string, number>
): MarketDataProvider {
if (csvContent && initialPrices) {
return new UnifiedMarketData(csvContent, initialPrices);
}
if (csvContent) {
return new CSVMarketDataProvider(csvContent);
}
return new MockPriceGenerator(initialPrices || { AAPL: 150.0, GOOGL: 140.0, MSFT: 380.0 });
}
'''

print(f"marketData.ts: {len(market_data_ts)} bytes")

private parseCSV(content: string) {

const headers = lines[0].split(',').map(h => h.trim().toLowerCase());

const symbolIdx = headers.indexOf('symbol');
const firmIdx = headers.indexOf('firm');

const targetIdx = headers.indexOf('target_price');
const dateIdx = headers.indexOf('date');

for (let i = 1; i < lines.length; i++) {
  const cols = this.parseLine(lines[i]);
  if (cols.length < headers.length) continue;

  const symbol = cols[symbolIdx]?.trim().toUpperCase();
  if (!symbol) continue;

  const rating: AnalystRating = {
    symbol,
    firm: cols[firmIdx]?.trim() || 'Unknown',
    rating: this.normalizeRating(cols[ratingIdx]?.trim() || 'hold'),
    targetPrice: Math.round(parseFloat(cols[targetIdx] || '0') * 100),
    date: cols[dateIdx]?.trim() || new Date().toISOString(),
  };

  if (!this.ratings.has(symbol)) {
    this.ratings.set(symbol, []);
    this.symbols.push(symbol);
  }
  this.ratings.get(symbol)!.push(rating);
}
}

private parseLine(line: string): string[] {
const result: string[] = [];
let current = '';
let inQuotes = false;

for (const char of line) {
  if (char === '"') {
    inQuotes = !inQuotes;
  } else if (char === ',' && !inQuotes) {
    result.push(current.trim());
    current = '';
  } else {
    current += char;
  }
}
result.push(current.trim());
return result;
}

private normalizeRating(r: string): AnalystRating['rating'] {
const map: Record<string, AnalystRating['rating']> = {
'buy': 'buy', 'b': 'buy',
'hold': 'hold', 'h': 'hold', 'neutral': 'hold',
'sell': 'sell', 's': 'sell',
'strong buy': 'strong_buy', 'strong_buy': 'strong_buy', 'sb': 'strong_buy',
'strong sell': 'strong_sell', 'strong_sell': 'strong_sell', 'ss': 'strong_sell',
};
return map[r.toLowerCase()] || 'hold';
}

async getQuotes(symbols: string[]): Promise<Quote[]> {
// In a real implementation, this would fetch from an API
// For simulation, we generate realistic quotes based on analyst targets
return symbols.map(sym => {
const ratings = this.ratings.get(sym) || [];
const avgTarget = ratings.length > 0
? ratings.reduce((s, r) => s + r.targetPrice, 0) / ratings.length
: 15000; // Default $150.00

  // Simulate current price near target with some variance
  const variance = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.1; // ±5%
  const price = Math.round(avgTarget * (1 + variance));
  
  return {
    symbol: sym,
    price,
    change: Math.round(price * (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.02),
    changePercent: parseFloat((Math.random() * 4 - 2).toFixed(2)),
    volume: Math.floor(Math.random() * 10000000) + 1000000,
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
  };
});
}

async getRatings(symbol: string): Promise<AnalystRating[]> {
return this.ratings.get(symbol.toUpperCase()) || [];
}

getAvailableSymbols(): string[] {
return [...this.symbols];
}
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Mock Price Generator — Realistic simulation for paper trading
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

export interface PriceModel {
drift: number; // Annualized expected return (decimal)
volatility: number; // Annualized volatility (decimal)
jumpProb: number; // Probability of jump per day
jumpSize: number; // Average jump size (decimal)
}

export class MockPriceGenerator implements MarketDataProvider {
private prices: Map<string, number> = new Map();
private models: Map<string, PriceModel> = new Map();
private lastUpdate: Map<string, number> = new Map();

constructor(initialPrices: Record<string, number>) {
Object.entries(initialPrices).forEach(([sym, price]) => {
this.prices.set(sym, Math.round(price * 100));
this.models.set(sym, {
drift: 0.08, // 8% annual return
volatility: 0.25, // 25% annual volatility
jumpProb: 0.02, // 2% daily jump probability
jumpSize: 0.05, // 5% average jump
});
this.lastUpdate.set(sym, Date.now());
});
}

async getQuotes(symbols: string[]): Promise<Quote[]> {
return symbols.map(sym => {
const currentPrice = this.prices.get(sym) || 10000;
const model = this.models.get(sym)!;
const lastTime = this.lastUpdate.get(sym) || Date.now();

  // Time since last update in trading days (approx)
  const daysElapsed = (Date.now() - lastTime) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24);
  
  // Geometric Brownian Motion step
  const dt = daysElapsed / 252; // Trading days per year
  const randomShock = this.gaussianRandom() * Math.sqrt(dt);
  const driftTerm = (model.drift - 0.5 * model.volatility ** 2) * dt;
  const volTerm = model.volatility * randomShock;
  
  let newPrice = currentPrice * Math.exp(driftTerm + volTerm);
  
  // Jump diffusion
  if (Math.random() < model.jumpProb * daysElapsed) {
    const jumpDir = Math.random() > 0.5 ? 1 : -1;
    newPrice *= (1 + jumpDir * model.jumpSize * Math.random());
  }
  
  newPrice = Math.max(1, Math.round(newPrice));
  const change = newPrice - currentPrice;
  
  this.prices.set(sym, newPrice);
  this.lastUpdate.set(sym, Date.now());
  
  return {
    symbol: sym,
    price: newPrice,
    change,
    changePercent: parseFloat(((change / currentPrice) * 100).toFixed(2)),
    volume: Math.floor(Math.random() * 10000000) + 1000000,
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
  };
});
}

async getRatings(symbol: string): Promise<AnalystRating[]> {
// Mock ratings for simulation
return [{
symbol: symbol.toUpperCase(),
firm: 'Mock Analytics',
rating: Math.random() > 0.5 ? 'buy' : 'hold',
targetPrice: Math.round((this.prices.get(symbol) || 10000) * (1 + (Math.random() - 0.3) * 0.2)),
date: new Date().toISOString(),
}];
}

getAvailableSymbols(): string[] {
return Array.from(this.prices.keys());
}

private gaussianRandom(): number {
// Box-Muller transform
const u1 = Math.random();
const u2 = Math.random();
return Math.sqrt(-2 * Math.log(u1)) * Math.cos(2 * Math.PI * u2);
}

setModel(symbol: string, model: PriceModel) {
this.models.set(symbol.toUpperCase(), model);
}
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Unified Market Data — Combines real ratings with simulated prices
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

export class UnifiedMarketData implements MarketDataProvider {
private csvProvider: CSVMarketDataProvider;
private mockGenerator: MockPriceGenerator;

constructor(csvContent: string, initialPrices: Record<string, number>) {
this.csvProvider = new CSVMarketDataProvider(csvContent);
this.mockGenerator = new MockPriceGenerator(initialPrices);
}

async getQuotes(symbols: string[]): Promise<Quote[]> {
// Use mock generator for prices, but enrich with analyst sentiment
const quotes = await this.mockGenerator.getQuotes(symbols);

return Promise.all(quotes.map(async q => {
  const ratings = await this.csvProvider.getRatings(q.symbol);
  if (ratings.length > 0) {
    // Adjust price slightly based on analyst consensus
    const buyCount = ratings.filter(r => r.rating.includes('buy')).length;
    const sellCount = ratings.filter(r => r.rating.includes('sell')).length;
    const sentiment = (buyCount - sellCount) / ratings.length;
    
    // Sentiment affects price by up to 2%
    const adjustment = 1 + sentiment * 0.02;
    q.price = Math.round(q.price * adjustment);
  }
  return q;
}));
}

async getRatings(symbol: string): Promise<AnalystRating[]> {
// Prefer real ratings, fall back to mock
const real = await this.csvProvider.getRatings(symbol);
return real.length > 0 ? real : this.mockGenerator.getRatings(symbol);
}

getAvailableSymbols(): string[] {
const real = this.csvProvider.getAvailableSymbols();
const mock = this.mockGenerator.getAvailableSymbols();
return [...new Set([...real, ...mock])];
}
}

// Factory function
export function getMarketData(
csvContent?: string,
initialPrices?: Record<string, number>
): MarketDataProvider {
if (csvContent && initialPrices) {
return new UnifiedMarketData(csvContent, initialPrices);
}
if (csvContent) {
return new CSVMarketDataProvider(csvContent);
}
return new MockPriceGenerator(initialPrices || { AAPL: 150.0, GOOGL: 140.0, MSFT: 380.0 });
}
'''

PHASE 2 (continued): Portfolio State Management

portfolio_ts = '''/**

portfolio.ts — Portfolio State Management for Trading Simulator
Cents-based arithmetic, invariant enforcement, secure execution wrapper.
All monetary values stored and computed in integer cents to avoid float drift.
*/
import { canonicalHash } from '../deep-human-nature-test/canonical.js';

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Types
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

export interface Position {
symbol: string;
shares: number; // Integer shares
avgCost: number; // In cents (average cost per share)
currentPrice: number; // In cents (last known price)
}

export interface Order {
id: string;
symbol: string;
side: 'buy' | 'sell';
shares: number; // Positive integer
orderType: 'market' | 'limit';
limitPrice?: number; // In cents (required for limit orders)
timestamp: string;
}

export interface Trade {
id: string;
orderId: string;
symbol: string;
side: 'buy' | 'sell';
shares: number;
price: number; // Execution price in cents
total: number; // Total value in cents (price * shares)
fees: number; // Transaction fees in cents
timestamp: string;
proof?: BoundProof; // Cryptographic proof of execution
}

export interface BoundProof {
hash: string;
signature: string;
algorithm: string;
timestamp: string;
payload: Record<string, unknown>;
}

export interface Portfolio {
cash: number; // Available cash in cents
positions: Position[];
trades: Trade[];
totalValue: number; // Computed: cash + sum(position values)
totalCost: number; // Total amount invested
unrealizedPnL: number;
realizedPnL: number;
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Invariant Enforcement (from src/money.ts patterns)
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

class InvariantError extends Error {
constructor(message: string) {
super(INVARIANT_VIOLATION: ${message});
this.name = 'InvariantError';
}
}

function assertInvariant(condition: boolean, message: string): void {
if (!condition) throw new InvariantError(message);
}

function cents(value: number): number {
// Ensure value is in whole cents
const rounded = Math.round(value);
assertInvariant(rounded === value, Value ${value} is not in whole cents);
return rounded;
}

function addCents(a: number, b: number): number {
return cents(a + b);
}

function subCents(a: number, b: number): number {
const result = a - b;
assertInvariant(result >= 0, Subtraction would result in negative cents: ${a} - ${b});
return cents(result);
}

function mulCents(a: number, b: number): number {
// a is cents, b is integer shares
return cents(a * b);
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Portfolio Manager
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

const DEFAULT_FEES_BPS = 35; // 0.35% per trade

export class PortfolioManager {
private portfolio: Portfolio;
private feeRate: number; // In basis points

constructor(initialCash: number = 10000000) { // $100,000.00 default
this.feeRate = DEFAULT_FEES_BPS;
this.portfolio = {
cash: cents(initialCash),
positions: [],
trades: [],
totalValue: cents(initialCash),
totalCost: 0,
unrealizedPnL: 0,
realizedPnL: 0,
};
}

getState(): Portfolio {
return { ...this.portfolio };
}

/**

Execute an order with validation, state update, and proof generation.
Wraps the existing secureExecute() pattern.
*/
async executeOrder(order: Order): Promise {
// Validate order
this.validateOrder(order);
// Get current price (in real system, this would come from market data)
const executionPrice = await this.getExecutionPrice(order);

// Calculate costs
const grossTotal = mulCents(executionPrice, order.shares);
const fees = cents(Math.round(grossTotal * this.feeRate / 10000));
const totalCost = addCents(grossTotal, fees);

// Check buying power for buys
if (order.side === 'buy') {
  assertInvariant(
    this.portfolio.cash >= totalCost,
    `Insufficient cash: ${this.portfolio.cash} < ${totalCost}`
  );
}

// Check position for sells
if (order.side === 'sell') {
  const position = this.portfolio.positions.find(p => p.symbol === order.symbol);
  assertInvariant(
    position && position.shares >= order.shares,
    `Insufficient shares: ${position?.shares || 0} < ${order.shares}`
  );
}

// Build trade
const trade: Trade = {
  id: this.generateId(),
  orderId: order.id,
  symbol: order.symbol,
  side: order.side,
  shares: order.shares,
  price: executionPrice,
  total: grossTotal,
  fees,
  timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
};

// Generate proof via secureExecute wrapper
trade.proof = await this.secureExecute(trade);

// Update portfolio state
this.updatePortfolio(trade);

return trade;
}

private validateOrder(order: Order): void {
assertInvariant(order.shares > 0, 'Order shares must be positive');
assertInvariant(order.shares === Math.floor(order.shares), 'Shares must be whole number');
assertInvariant(
['buy', 'sell'].includes(order.side),
Invalid side: ${order.side}
);

if (order.orderType === 'limit') {
  assertInvariant(
    order.limitPrice !== undefined && order.limitPrice > 0,
    'Limit orders require positive limitPrice'
  );
}
}

private async getExecutionPrice(order: Order): Promise {
// In real implementation, fetch from market data provider
// For simulation, use a deterministic price based on symbol hash
const basePrice = this.hashToPrice(order.symbol);
const variance = (Math.sin(Date.now() / 10000) + 1) * 0.02; // ±2% variance
return cents(Math.round(basePrice * (1 + variance)));
}

private hashToPrice(symbol: string): number {
// Deterministic pseudo-price from symbol name
let hash = 0;
for (let i = 0; i < symbol.length; i++) {
hash = ((hash << 5) - hash) + symbol.charCodeAt(i);
hash |= 0;
}
return 5000 + (Math.abs(hash) % 45000); // $50.00 to $500.00
}

private async secureExecute(trade: Trade): Promise {
// Wrap trade execution in cryptographic proof
// This mirrors the secureExecute() pattern from tradepro_v2_verified.html
const payload = {
tradeId: trade.id,
symbol: trade.symbol,
side: trade.side,
shares: trade.shares,
price: trade.price,
total: trade.total,
fees: trade.fees,
timestamp: trade.timestamp,
};

const hash = await canonicalHash(payload);

// In production, this would sign with the trader's private key
// For simulation, we generate a deterministic mock signature
const signature = await this.mockSign(hash);

return {
  hash,
  signature,
  algorithm: 'SHA-256-Ed25519',
  timestamp: trade.timestamp,
  payload,
};
}

private async mockSign(hash: string): Promise {
// Deterministic mock signature for simulation
// In production: use tweetnacl or Web Crypto with real keys
const encoder = new TextEncoder();
const data = encoder.encode(hash + 'mock-secret-seed');
const digest = await crypto.subtle.digest('SHA-256', data);
return Array.from(new Uint8Array(digest))
.map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0'))
.join('');
}

private updatePortfolio(trade: Trade): void {
if (trade.side === 'buy') {
// Deduct cash
this.portfolio.cash = subCents(this.portfolio.cash, addCents(trade.total, trade.fees));

  // Update or create position
  const existing = this.portfolio.positions.find(p => p.symbol === trade.symbol);
  if (existing) {
    const totalShares = existing.shares + trade.shares;
    const totalCost = addCents(
      mulCents(existing.avgCost, existing.shares),
      mulCents(trade.price, trade.shares)
    );
    existing.shares = totalShares;
    existing.avgCost = cents(Math.round(totalCost / totalShares));
    existing.currentPrice = trade.price;
  } else {
    this.portfolio.positions.push({
      symbol: trade.symbol,
      shares: trade.shares,
      avgCost: trade.price,
      currentPrice: trade.price,
    });
  }
  
  this.portfolio.totalCost = addCents(this.portfolio.totalCost, addCents(trade.total, trade.fees));
} else {
  // Sell: add cash, reduce position, realize P&L
  const position = this.portfolio.positions.find(p => p.symbol === trade.symbol)!;
  const costBasis = mulCents(position.avgCost, trade.shares);
  const proceeds = subCents(trade.total, trade.fees);
  const pnl = subCents(proceeds, costBasis);
  
  this.portfolio.realizedPnL = addCents(this.portfolio.realizedPnL, pnl);
  this.portfolio.cash = addCents(this.portfolio.cash, proceeds);
  
  position.shares -= trade.shares;
  if (position.shares === 0) {
    this.portfolio.positions = this.portfolio.positions.filter(p => p.symbol !== trade.symbol);
  }
}

// Record trade
this.portfolio.trades.push(trade);

// Recalculate totals
this.recalculate();
}

private recalculate(): void {
const positionValue = this.portfolio.positions.reduce((sum, p) => {
return addCents(sum, mulCents(p.currentPrice, p.shares));
}, 0);

this.portfolio.totalValue = addCents(this.portfolio.cash, positionValue);

// Unrealized P&L
this.portfolio.unrealizedPnL = this.portfolio.positions.reduce((sum, p) => {
  const costBasis = mulCents(p.avgCost, p.shares);
  const marketValue = mulCents(p.currentPrice, p.shares);
  return sum + (marketValue - costBasis);
}, 0);
}

/**

Update current prices for all positions (called on price tick).
*/
updatePrices(prices: Record<string, number>): void {
for (const pos of this.portfolio.positions) {
if (prices[pos.symbol] !== undefined) {
pos.currentPrice = cents(prices[pos.symbol]);
}
}
this.recalculate();
}
/**

Get portfolio statistics.
*/
getStats(): {
cash: number;
invested: number;
totalValue: number;
totalReturn: number;
totalReturnPercent: number;
tradeCount: number;
} {
const invested = this.portfolio.positions.reduce((s, p) =>
addCents(s, mulCents(p.avgCost, p.shares)), 0
);
const totalReturn = addCents(this.portfolio.realizedPnL, this.portfolio.unrealizedPnL);
const totalReturnPercent = this.portfolio.totalCost > 0
? parseFloat(((totalReturn / this.portfolio.totalCost) * 100).toFixed(2))
: 0;
return {
  cash: this.portfolio.cash,
  invested,
  totalValue: this.portfolio.totalValue,
  totalReturn,
  totalReturnPercent,
  tradeCount: this.portfolio.trades.length,
};
}

private generateId(): string {
return trd_${Date.now()}_${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 8)};
}
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Export utilities
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

export function formatCents(cents: number): string {
const dollars = cents / 100;
return $${dollars.toFixed(2)};
}

export function formatPercent(decimal: number): string {
const sign = decimal >= 0 ? '+' : '';
return ${sign}${decimal.toFixed(2)}%;
}
'''

print(f"portfolio.ts: {len(portfolio_ts)} bytes")

interface PortfolioPanelProps {

export const PortfolioPanel: React.FC = ({ portfolio }) => {

const totalReturn = portfolio.realizedPnL + portfolio.unrealizedPnL;
const totalReturnPct = totalCost > 0 ? (totalReturn / totalCost) * 100 : 0;

return (

  <div className="stats-grid">

      <div className="stat-label">Invested</div>
      <div className="stat-value">{formatCents(totalCost)}</div>

    <div className={`stat-card ${totalReturn >= 0 ? 'positive' : 'negative'}`}>

      </div>

            <th>Current</th>
            <th>P&L</th>

          {portfolio.positions.map(pos => {
            const marketValue = pos.currentPrice * pos.shares;

                <td className="symbol">{pos.symbol}</td>
                <td>{pos.shares}</td>
                <td>{formatCents(pos.avgCost)}</td>
                <td>{formatCents(pos.currentPrice)}</td>
                <td className={pnl >= 0 ? 'positive' : 'negative'}>
                  {formatCents(pnl)} ({formatPercent(pnlPct)})
                </td>
              </tr>
            );
          })}
        </tbody>
      </table>
    )}
  </div>
</div>
);
};

order_form_tsx = '''import React, { useState } from 'react';

File 5: TradeHistory.tsx
trade_history_tsx = '''import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { Trade, formatCents } from '../../lib/portfolio';

interface TradeHistoryProps {
trades: Trade[];
}

export const TradeHistory: React.FC = ({ trades }) => {
const [expandedTrade, setExpandedTrade] = useState<string | null>(null);

if (trades.length === 0) {
return (


Trade History

No trades executed


);
}
return (


Trade History ({trades.length})
  <div className="trade-list">
    {trades.slice().reverse().map(trade => (
      <div key={trade.id} className={`trade-card ${trade.side}`}>
        <div 
          className="trade-header"
          onClick={() => setExpandedTrade(expandedTrade === trade.id ? null : trade.id)}
        >
          <div className="trade-main">
            <span className={`badge ${trade.side}`}>{trade.side.toUpperCase()}</span>
            <span className="symbol">{trade.symbol}</span>
            <span className="shares">{trade.shares} shares</span>
          </div>
          <div className="trade-summary">
            <span className="price">{formatCents(trade.price)}</span>
            <span className="total">{formatCents(trade.total)}</span>
            {trade.proof && (
              <span className="proof-badge">🔒</span>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
        
        {expandedTrade === trade.id && trade.proof && (
          <div className="trade-details">
            <div className="detail-row">
              <span className="label">Hash</span>
              <span className="value truncate">{trade.proof.hash}</span>
            </div>
            <div className="detail-row">
              <span className="label">Signature</span>
              <span className="value truncate">{trade.proof.signature.slice(0, 48)}...</span>
            </div>
            <div className="detail-row">
              <span className="label">Algorithm</span>
              <span className="value">{trade.proof.algorithm}</span>
            </div>
            <div className="detail-row">
              <span className="label">Fees</span>
              <span className="value">{formatCents(trade.fees)}</span>
            </div>
            <div className="detail-row">
              <span className="label">Timestamp</span>
              <span className="value">{new Date(trade.timestamp).toLocaleString()}</span>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    ))}
  </div>
</div>
);
};
'''

File 6: PriceChart.tsx (lightweight SVG-based)
price_chart_tsx = '''import React, { useMemo } from 'react';

interface PriceChartProps {
data: { time: string; price: number }[];
symbol: string;
color?: string;
}

export const PriceChart: React.FC = ({
data,
symbol,
color = '#00d4ff'
}) => {
const { path, min, max, viewBox } = useMemo(() => {
if (data.length < 2) return { path: '', min: 0, max: 0, viewBox: '0 0 100 100' };

const prices = data.map(d => d.price);
const min = Math.min(...prices);
const max = Math.max(...prices);
const range = max - min || 1;

const width = 600;
const height = 200;
const padding = 10;

const points = data.map((d, i) => {
  const x = padding + (i / (data.length - 1)) * (width - 2 * padding);
  const y = height - padding - ((d.price - min) / range) * (height - 2 * padding);
  return `${x},${y}`;
});

const path = `M ${points.join(' L ')}`;

return {
  path,
  min,
  max,
  viewBox: `0 0 ${width} ${height}`,
};
}, [data]);

if (data.length < 2) {
return (


{symbol}

Insufficient data


);
}
const currentPrice = data[data.length - 1].price;
const startPrice = data[0].price;
const change = ((currentPrice - startPrice) / startPrice) * 100;

return (



{symbol}

<span className={change ${change >= 0 ? 'positive' : 'negative'}}>
{change >= 0 ? '+' : ''}{change.toFixed(2)}%

  <svg viewBox={viewBox} className="chart-svg">
    <defs>
      <linearGradient id={`gradient-${symbol}`} x1="0" y1="0" x2="0" y2="1">
        <stop offset="0%" stopColor={color} stopOpacity="0.3" />
        <stop offset="100%" stopColor={color} stopOpacity="0" />
      </linearGradient>
    </defs>
    
    {/* Area fill */}
    <path
      d={`${path} L 600,200 L 0,200 Z`}
      fill={`url(#gradient-${symbol})`}
    />
    
    {/* Line */}
    <path
      d={path}
      fill="none"
      stroke={color}
      strokeWidth="2"
      strokeLinecap="round"
      strokeLinejoin="round"
    />
    
    {/* Current price dot */}
    {data.length > 0 && (
      <circle
        cx={600 - 10}
        cy={200 - 10 - ((currentPrice - min) / (max - min || 1)) * 180}
        r="4"
        fill={color}
      />
    )}
  </svg>
  
  <div className="chart-footer">
    <span>Low: ${(min / 100).toFixed(2)}</span>
    <span>High: ${(max / 100).toFixed(2)}</span>
  </div>
</div>
);
};
'''

PHASE 2: WEB-BASED STOCK TRADING SIMULATOR

File 1: marketData.ts — Data Adapter Layer
marketData_ts = '''/**

marketData.ts — Data Adapter Layer for Stock Trading Simulator
Provides unified market data combining real analyst ratings (CSV)
with realistic price simulation for trading.
*/
export interface Stock {
symbol: string;
name: string;
sector: string;
}

export interface Quote {
symbol: string;
price: number; // current price in dollars
change: number; // dollar change
changePercent: number;
volume: number;
timestamp: string;
bid: number;
ask: number;
}

export interface AnalystRating {
symbol: string;
analyst: string;
rating: 'Buy' | 'Hold' | 'Sell' | 'Strong Buy' | 'Strong Sell';
targetPrice: number;
date: string;
}

export interface MarketDataProvider {
getQuotes(symbols: string[]): Promise<Quote[]>;
getAnalystRatings(symbol: string): Promise<AnalystRating[]>;
getAvailableStocks(): Stock[];
}

// ============================================================
// CSV Market Data Provider — parses aapl_analyst_ratings.csv
// ============================================================

export class CSVMarketDataProvider implements MarketDataProvider {
private ratings: AnalystRating[] = [];
private stocks: Stock[] = [
{ symbol: 'AAPL', name: 'Apple Inc.', sector: 'Technology' },
{ symbol: 'MSFT', name: 'Microsoft Corp.', sector: 'Technology' },
{ symbol: 'GOOGL', name: 'Alphabet Inc.', sector: 'Technology' },
{ symbol: 'AMZN', name: 'Amazon.com Inc.', sector: 'Consumer Cyclical' },
{ symbol: 'TSLA', name: 'Tesla Inc.', sector: 'Consumer Cyclical' },
{ symbol: 'NVDA', name: 'NVIDIA Corp.', sector: 'Technology' },
{ symbol: 'META', name: 'Meta Platforms', sector: 'Technology' },
{ symbol: 'JPM', name: 'JPMorgan Chase', sector: 'Financial' },
{ symbol: 'JNJ', name: 'Johnson & Johnson', sector: 'Healthcare' },
{ symbol: 'V', name: 'Visa Inc.', sector: 'Financial' },
];

constructor(csvContent?: string) {
if (csvContent) {
this.parseCSV(csvContent);
}
}

private parseCSV(csv: string) {
const lines = csv.trim().split('\n');
const headers = lines[0].split(',').map(h => h.trim().replace(/^"|"$/g, ''));

for (let i = 1; i < lines.length; i++) {
  const values = this.parseLine(lines[i]);
  if (values.length >= headers.length) {
    this.ratings.push({
      symbol: values[0] || 'AAPL',
      analyst: values[1] || 'Unknown',
      rating: this.normalizeRating(values[2]),
      targetPrice: parseFloat(values[3]) || 0,
      date: values[4] || new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0],
    });
  }
}
}

private parseLine(line: string): string[] {
const result: string[] = [];
let current = '';
let inQuotes = false;

for (const char of line) {
  if (char === '"') {
    inQuotes = !inQuotes;
  } else if (char === ',' && !inQuotes) {
    result.push(current.trim());
    current = '';
  } else {
    current += char;
  }
}
result.push(current.trim());
return result;
}

private normalizeRating(r: string): AnalystRating['rating'] {
const map: Record<string, AnalystRating['rating']> = {
'Buy': 'Buy', 'Hold': 'Hold', 'Sell': 'Sell',
'Strong Buy': 'Strong Buy', 'Strong Sell': 'Strong Sell',
'Overweight': 'Buy', 'Underweight': 'Sell', 'Equal Weight': 'Hold',
'Outperform': 'Buy', 'Underperform': 'Sell', 'Market Perform': 'Hold',
};
return map[r?.trim()] || 'Hold';
}

async getQuotes(symbols: string[]): Promise<Quote[]> {
// In real implementation, this would fetch from an API
// For simulation, generate realistic quotes
return symbols.map(sym => this.generateQuote(sym));
}

private generateQuote(symbol: string): Quote {
const basePrice = this.getBasePrice(symbol);
const volatility = 0.02; // 2% daily volatility
const change = basePrice * volatility * (Math.random() - 0.5) * 2;

return {
  symbol,
  price: Math.round((basePrice + change) * 100) / 100,
  change: Math.round(change * 100) / 100,
  changePercent: Math.round((change / basePrice) * 10000) / 100,
  volume: Math.floor(Math.random() * 50000000) + 1000000,
  timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
  bid: Math.round((basePrice + change - 0.01) * 100) / 100,
  ask: Math.round((basePrice + change + 0.01) * 100) / 100,
};
}

private getBasePrice(symbol: string): number {
const prices: Record<string, number> = {
AAPL: 175.50, MSFT: 380.20, GOOGL: 142.80, AMZN: 178.30,
TSLA: 245.60, NVDA: 485.90, META: 505.40, JPM: 198.70,
JNJ: 152.30, V: 278.90,
};
return prices[symbol] || 100.00;
}

async getAnalystRatings(symbol: string): Promise<AnalystRating[]> {
return this.ratings.filter(r => r.symbol === symbol);
}

getAvailableStocks(): Stock[] {
return this.stocks;
}
}

// ============================================================
// Mock Price Generator — realistic price movements
// ============================================================

export class MockPriceGenerator {
private prices: Map<string, number> = new Map();
private readonly drift = 0.0001; // slight upward drift
private readonly volatility = 0.015; // 1.5% per tick

constructor(initialPrices: Record<string, number>) {
Object.entries(initialPrices).forEach(([sym, price]) => {
this.prices.set(sym, price);
});
}

tick(symbol: string): Quote {
let price = this.prices.get(symbol) || 100.00;

// Geometric Brownian Motion approximation
const dt = 1 / 252; // one trading day
const randomShock = this.volatility * Math.sqrt(dt) * this.gaussianRandom();
const driftTerm = this.drift * dt;

price = price * Math.exp(driftTerm + randomShock);
price = Math.round(price * 100) / 100;

this.prices.set(symbol, price);

const prevPrice = price / (1 + driftTerm + randomShock);
const change = price - prevPrice;

return {
  symbol,
  price,
  change: Math.round(change * 100) / 100,
  changePercent: Math.round((change / prevPrice) * 10000) / 100,
  volume: Math.floor(Math.random() * 10000000) + 500000,
  timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
  bid: Math.round((price - 0.01) * 100) / 100,
  ask: Math.round((price + 0.01) * 100) / 100,
};
}

private gaussianRandom(): number {
// Box-Muller transform
const u1 = Math.random();
const u2 = Math.random();
return Math.sqrt(-2.0 * Math.log(u1)) * Math.cos(2.0 * Math.PI * u2);
}

getPrice(symbol: string): number {
return this.prices.get(symbol) || 100.00;
}
}

// ============================================================
// Unified Market Data Function
// ============================================================

export interface UnifiedMarketData {
quote: Quote;
ratings: AnalystRating[];
stock: Stock;
}

export async function getMarketData(
symbol: string,
provider: MarketDataProvider
): Promise {
const [quotes, ratings, stocks] = await Promise.all([
provider.getQuotes([symbol]),
provider.getAnalystRatings(symbol),
Promise.resolve(provider.getAvailableStocks()),
]);

return {
quote: quotes[0],
ratings,
stock: stocks.find(s => s.symbol === symbol) || { symbol, name: symbol, sector: 'Unknown' },
};
}
'''

print(f"marketData.ts: {len(marketData_ts)} bytes")

// ============================================================
// Mock Price Generator — realistic price movements

export class MockPriceGenerator {
private prices: Map<string, number> = new Map();
private readonly drift = 0.0001; // slight upward drift
private readonly volatility = 0.015; // 1.5% per tick

constructor(initialPrices: Record<string, number>) {

});
}

tick(symbol: string): Quote {

  changePercent: Math.round((change / prevPrice) * 10000) / 100,

  timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
  bid: Math.round((price - 0.01) * 100) / 100,
  ask: Math.round((price + 0.01) * 100) / 100,
};

const u2 = Math.random();

}

getPrice(symbol: string): number {

portfolio_panel_tsx = '''/**

PortfolioPanel.tsx — Displays holdings, values, and P&L
*/
import React from 'react';
import { Portfolio, Position } from '../../lib/portfolio';

interface PortfolioPanelProps {
portfolio: Portfolio;
}

const formatCents = (cents: number): string => {
const abs = Math.abs(cents);
const sign = cents < 0 ? '-' : '';
return ${sign}$${(abs / 100).toFixed(2)};
};

const formatChange = (cents: number): string => {
const pct = cents >= 0 ? '+' : '';
return ${pct}${(cents / 100).toFixed(2)};
};

export const PortfolioPanel: React.FC = ({ portfolio }) => {
const totalValue = portfolio.totalValueCents / 100;
const cash = portfolio.cashCents / 100;
const pnl = portfolio.totalPnlCents / 100;
const pnlPositive = portfolio.totalPnlCents >= 0;

return (


Portfolio
  <div style={styles.summary}>
    <div style={styles.summaryItem}>
      <div style={styles.summaryLabel}>Total Value</div>
      <div style={styles.summaryValue}>${totalValue.toFixed(2)}</div>
    </div>
    <div style={styles.summaryItem}>
      <div style={styles.summaryLabel}>Cash</div>
      <div style={styles.summaryValue}>${cash.toFixed(2)}</div>
    </div>
    <div style={styles.summaryItem}>
      <div style={styles.summaryLabel}>P&L</div>
      <div style={{...styles.summaryValue, color: pnlPositive ? '#00ff88' : '#ff3333'}}>
        {pnlPositive ? '+' : ''}${pnl.toFixed(2)}
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>

  <h3 style={styles.subHeader}>Positions</h3>
  {portfolio.positions.length === 0 ? (
    <div style={styles.empty}>No positions</div>
  ) : (
    <table style={styles.table}>
      <thead>
        <tr>
          <th style={styles.th}>Symbol</th>
          <th style={styles.th}>Qty</th>
          <th style={styles.th}>Avg Cost</th>
          <th style={styles.th}>Current</th>
          <th style={styles.th}>P&L</th>
        </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
        {portfolio.positions.map((pos: Position) => {
          const pnlCents = (pos.currentPriceCents - pos.avgCostCents) * pos.quantity;
          const pnlPct = ((pos.currentPriceCents - pos.avgCostCents) / pos.avgCostCents) * 100;
          const positive = pnlCents >= 0;
          
          return (
            <tr key={pos.symbol} style={styles.tr}>
              <td style={styles.td}><strong>{pos.symbol}</strong></td>
              <td style={styles.td}>{pos.quantity}</td>
              <td style={styles.td}>${(pos.avgCostCents / 100).toFixed(2)}</td>
              <td style={styles.td}>${(pos.currentPriceCents / 100).toFixed(2)}</td>
              <td style={{...styles.td, color: positive ? '#00ff88' : '#ff3333'}}>
                {positive ? '+' : ''}{pnlPct.toFixed(1)}%
              </td>
            </tr>
          );
        })}
      </tbody>
    </table>
  )}
</div>
);
};

const styles: Record<string, React.CSSProperties> = {
container: {
background: '#111111',
border: '1px solid #333333',
borderRadius: '12px',
padding: '24px',
color: '#e0e0e0',
fontFamily: "'SF Pro Display', -apple-system, sans-serif",
},
header: {
fontSize: '18px',
fontWeight: 700,

},

gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(3, 1fr)',

},

textAlign: 'center',
},

},

},

File 4: OrderForm.tsx
order_form_tsx = '''/**

OrderForm.tsx — Buy/sell order entry form with validation
*/
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { Order } from '../../lib/portfolio';
import { Stock } from '../../lib/marketData';

interface OrderFormProps {
stocks: Stock[];
currentPrices: Record<string, number>;
cashCents: number;
positions: { symbol: string; quantity: number }[];
onSubmit: (order: Order) => void;
}

export const OrderForm: React.FC = ({
stocks,
currentPrices,
cashCents,
positions,
onSubmit,
}) => {
const [symbol, setSymbol] = useState('');
const [side, setSide] = useState<'buy' | 'sell'>('buy');
const [quantity, setQuantity] = useState('');
const [orderType, setOrderType] = useState<'market' | 'limit'>('market');
const [limitPrice, setLimitPrice] = useState('');
const [error, setError] = useState('');

const selectedStock = stocks.find(s => s.symbol === symbol);
const currentPrice = symbol ? currentPrices[symbol] || 0 : 0;
const qty = parseInt(quantity, 10) || 0;
const estimatedTotal = currentPrice * qty;
const canAfford = estimatedTotal * 100 <= cashCents;

const position = positions.find(p => p.symbol === symbol);
const canSell = position && position.quantity >= qty;

const handleSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
e.preventDefault();
setError('');

if (!symbol) { setError('Select a stock'); return; }
if (!qty || qty <= 0) { setError('Enter valid quantity'); return; }
if (qty > 1000000) { setError('Quantity too large'); return; }

if (side === 'buy' && !canAfford) {
  setError(`Insufficient funds: need $${estimatedTotal.toFixed(2)}`);
  return;
}
if (side === 'sell' && !canSell) {
  setError(`Insufficient shares: have ${position?.quantity || 0}`);
  return;
}

const order: Order = {
  id: `ORD-${Date.now()}`,
  symbol,
  side,
  quantity: qty,
  orderType,
  limitPriceCents: orderType === 'limit' ? Math.round(parseFloat(limitPrice) * 100) : undefined,
  timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
};

onSubmit(order);
setQuantity('');
setLimitPrice('');
};

return (


Place Order
  <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
    <div style={styles.sideToggle}>
      <button
        type="button"
        style={{...styles.sideBtn, ...(side === 'buy' ? styles.sideBuyActive : {})}}
        onClick={() => setSide('buy')}
      >
        BUY
      </button>
      <button
        type="button"
        style={{...styles.sideBtn, ...(side === 'sell' ? styles.sideSellActive : {})}}
        onClick={() => setSide('sell')}
      >
        SELL
      </button>
    </div>

    <div style={styles.field}>
      <label style={styles.label}>Stock</label>
      <select
        style={styles.select}
        value={symbol}
        onChange={e => setSymbol(e.target.value)}
      >
        <option value="">Select...</option>
        {stocks.map(s => (
          <option key={s.symbol} value={s.symbol}>
            {s.symbol} — {s.name}
          </option>
        ))}
      </select>
    </div>

    {symbol && (
      <div style={styles.priceInfo}>
        Current: <strong>${currentPrice.toFixed(2)}</strong>
        {selectedStock && (
          <span style={styles.sector}> {selectedStock.sector}</span>
        )}
      </div>
    )}

    <div style={styles.field}>
      <label style={styles.label}>Quantity</label>
      <input
        type="number"
        style={styles.input}
        value={quantity}
        onChange={e => setQuantity(e.target.value)}
        min={1}
        placeholder="0"
      />
    </div>

    <div style={styles.field}>
      <label style={styles.label}>Order Type</label>
      <div style={styles.typeToggle}>
        <button
          type="button"
          style={{...styles.typeBtn, ...(orderType === 'market' ? styles.typeActive : {})}}
          onClick={() => setOrderType('market')}
        >
          Market
        </button>
        <button
          type="button"
          style={{...styles.typeBtn, ...(orderType === 'limit' ? styles.typeActive : {})}}
          onClick={() => setOrderType('limit')}
        >
          Limit
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>

    {orderType === 'limit' && (
      <div style={styles.field}>
        <label style={styles.label}>Limit Price ($)</label>
        <input
          type="number"
          step="0.01"
          style={styles.input}
          value={limitPrice}
          onChange={e => setLimitPrice(e.target.value)}
          placeholder="0.00"
        />
      </div>
    )}

    {qty > 0 && (
      <div style={styles.estimate}>
        Estimated total: <strong>${estimatedTotal.toFixed(2)}</strong>
        {side === 'buy' && (
          <span style={{color: canAfford ? '#00ff88' : '#ff3333', marginLeft: 8}}>
            {canAfford ? '✓' : '✗ Insufficient funds'}
          </span>
        )}
        {side === 'sell' && (
          <span style={{color: canSell ? '#00ff88' : '#ff3333', marginLeft: 8}}>
            {canSell ? '✓' : '✗ Insufficient shares'}
          </span>
        )}
      </div>
    )}

    {error && <div style={styles.error}>{error}</div>}

    <button type="submit" style={styles.submit}>
      {side === 'buy' ? 'Buy' : 'Sell'} {symbol || '...'}
    </button>
  </form>
</div>
);
};

market_data_ts = '''/**

marketData.ts — Data Adapter Layer
Provides unified market data combining:
CSV analyst ratings (CSVMarketDataProvider)
Realistic mock price generation (MockPriceGenerator)
All prices use cents-based integer arithmetic (Money pattern).
*/
export interface Stock {
symbol: string;
name: string;
sector: string;
}

export interface Quote {
symbol: string;
price: number; // cents
change: number; // cents
changePercent: number;
volume: number;
timestamp: string;
}

export interface AnalystRating {
symbol: string;
analyst: string;
rating: 'buy' | 'hold' | 'sell';
targetPrice: number; // cents
date: string;
}

export interface MarketDataProvider {
getQuote(symbol: string): Promise;
getQuotes(symbols: string[]): Promise<Quote[]>;
getAnalystRatings(symbol: string): Promise<AnalystRating[]>;
getAllSymbols(): string[];
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// CSV Market Data Provider — parses aapl_analyst_ratings.csv
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

export class CSVMarketDataProvider implements MarketDataProvider {
private ratings: Map<string, AnalystRating[]> = new Map();
private symbols: string[] = [];

constructor(csvText: string) {
this.parseCSV(csvText);
}

private parseCSV(csvText: string) {
const lines = csvText.trim().split('\n');
const headers = lines[0].split(',').map(h => h.trim().toLowerCase());

for (let i = 1; i < lines.length; i++) {
  const values = lines[i].split(',').map(v => v.trim());
  if (values.length < headers.length) continue;
  
  const row: Record<string, string> = {};
  headers.forEach((h, idx) => row[h] = values[idx]);
  
  const symbol = row['symbol'] || row['ticker'] || '';
  if (!symbol) continue;
  
  const rating: AnalystRating = {
    symbol: symbol.toUpperCase(),
    analyst: row['analyst'] || row['firm'] || 'Unknown',
    rating: this.normalizeRating(row['rating'] || row['recommendation'] || ''),
    targetPrice: this.parsePrice(row['target_price'] || row['target'] || '0'),
    date: row['date'] || new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0],
  };
  
  if (!this.ratings.has(rating.symbol)) {
    this.ratings.set(rating.symbol, []);
    this.symbols.push(rating.symbol);
  }
  this.ratings.get(rating.symbol)!.push(rating);
}
}

private normalizeRating(r: string): 'buy' | 'hold' | 'sell' {
const lower = r.toLowerCase();
if (lower.includes('buy') || lower.includes('overweight') || lower.includes('outperform')) return 'buy';
if (lower.includes('sell') || lower.includes('underweight') || lower.includes('underperform')) return 'sell';
return 'hold';
}

private parsePrice(p: string): number {
const cleaned = p.replace(/[$,]/g, '');
const floatVal = parseFloat(cleaned);
return Math.round(floatVal * 100); // Convert to cents
}

async getQuote(symbol: string): Promise {
// Fallback: generate mock quote if no CSV data
return this.generateMockQuote(symbol);
}

async getQuotes(symbols: string[]): Promise<Quote[]> {
return Promise.all(symbols.map(s => this.getQuote(s)));
}

async getAnalystRatings(symbol: string): Promise<AnalystRating[]> {
return this.ratings.get(symbol.toUpperCase()) || [];
}

getAllSymbols(): string[] {
return [...this.symbols];
}

private generateMockQuote(symbol: string): Quote {
const basePrice = this.hashToPrice(symbol);
const volatility = 0.02;
const change = Math.round(basePrice * volatility * (Math.random() - 0.5));
return {
symbol,
price: basePrice + change,
change,
changePercent: Number((change / basePrice * 100).toFixed(2)),
volume: Math.floor(Math.random() * 10000000),
timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
};
}

private hashToPrice(symbol: string): number {
// Deterministic base price from symbol hash
let hash = 0;
for (let i = 0; i < symbol.length; i++) {
hash = ((hash << 5) - hash) + symbol.charCodeAt(i);
hash |= 0;
}
return 5000 + Math.abs(hash % 45000); // $50.00 - $500.00 in cents
}
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Mock Price Generator — realistic simulation prices
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

export class MockPriceGenerator {
private prices: Map<string, number> = new Map();
private readonly symbols = ['AAPL', 'GOOGL', 'MSFT', 'AMZN', 'TSLA', 'META', 'NVDA', 'NFLX'];

constructor() {
// Initialize with deterministic base prices
this.symbols.forEach(sym => {
this.prices.set(sym, this.hashToPrice(sym));
});
}

generateQuote(symbol: string): Quote {
const currentPrice = this.prices.get(symbol) || this.hashToPrice(symbol);
const drift = 0.001; // 0.1% mean reversion
const volatility = 0.015; // 1.5% volatility

const change = Math.round(currentPrice * (drift + volatility * (Math.random() - 0.5)));
const newPrice = Math.max(100, currentPrice + change); // Floor at $1.00

this.prices.set(symbol, newPrice);

return {
  symbol,
  price: newPrice,
  change,
  changePercent: Number((change / currentPrice * 100).toFixed(2)),
  volume: Math.floor(Math.random() * 5000000) + 1000000,
  timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
};
}

generateQuotes(symbols?: string[]): Quote[] {
const targets = symbols || this.symbols;
return targets.map(s => this.generateQuote(s));
}

getSymbols(): string[] {
return [...this.symbols];
}

private hashToPrice(symbol: string): number {
let hash = 0;
for (let i = 0; i < symbol.length; i++) {
hash = ((hash << 5) - hash) + symbol.charCodeAt(i);
hash |= 0;
}
return 10000 + Math.abs(hash % 40000); // $100.00 - $500.00 in cents
}
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Unified Market Data API
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

export interface UnifiedMarketData {
quote: Quote;
ratings: AnalystRating[];
consensusRating: 'buy' | 'hold' | 'sell' | 'unknown';
averageTarget: number | null; // cents
}

export async function getMarketData(
symbol: string,
csvProvider?: CSVMarketDataProvider
): Promise {
const mockGen = new MockPriceGenerator();
const quote = csvProvider
? await csvProvider.getQuote(symbol)
: mockGen.generateQuote(symbol);

const ratings = csvProvider
? await csvProvider.getAnalystRatings(symbol)
: [];

// Compute consensus
let consensusRating: 'buy' | 'hold' | 'sell' | 'unknown' = 'unknown';
let averageTarget: number | null = null;

if (ratings.length > 0) {
const buyCount = ratings.filter(r => r.rating === 'buy').length;
const sellCount = ratings.filter(r => r.rating === 'sell').length;
const holdCount = ratings.filter(r => r.rating === 'hold').length;

if (buyCount > sellCount && buyCount > holdCount) consensusRating = 'buy';
else if (sellCount > buyCount && sellCount > holdCount) consensusRating = 'sell';
else consensusRating = 'hold';

const targets = ratings.map(r => r.targetPrice).filter(p => p > 0);
if (targets.length > 0) {
  averageTarget = Math.round(targets.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / targets.length);
}
}

return {
quote,
ratings,
consensusRating,
averageTarget,
};
}
'''

print(f"marketData.ts: {len(market_data_ts)} bytes")
