portfolio_ts = '''/**

portfolio.ts — Portfolio State Management
Cents-based arithmetic following money.ts patterns.
All monetary values stored as integers (cents).
Invariant: balance >= 0, position.quantity >= 0 at all times.
Every trade routes through secureExecute() for verification binding.
*/
import { canonical, canonicalHash } from '../deep-human-nature-test/canonical.js';

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Types
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

export interface Position {
symbol: string;
quantity: number; // whole shares
avgCost: number; // cents per share
currentPrice: number; // cents per share (last known)
}

export interface Order {
id: string;
symbol: string;
side: 'buy' | 'sell';
quantity: number;
price: number; // cents per share (limit) or 0 for market
type: 'market' | 'limit';
timestamp: string;
status: 'pending' | 'filled' | 'rejected';
}

export interface Trade {
id: string;
orderId: string;
symbol: string;
side: 'buy' | 'sell';
quantity: number;
price: number; // cents per share (execution price)
total: number; // cents (quantity * price)
timestamp: string;
proof?: BoundProof;
}

export interface BoundProof {
hash: string;
signature: string;
publicKey: string;
timestamp: string;
algorithm: string;
}

export interface Portfolio {
cash: number; // cents
positions: Position[];
trades: Trade[];
totalValue: number; // cents (cash + position values)
dayPnl: number; // cents
totalPnl: number; // cents
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Money arithmetic — invariant enforcement
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

export class Money {
readonly cents: number;

constructor(cents: number) {
if (!Number.isInteger(cents)) {
throw new Error(Money invariant violated: ${cents} is not an integer);
}
this.cents = cents;
}

static fromDollars(dollars: number): Money {
return new Money(Math.round(dollars * 100));
}

toDollars(): number {
return this.cents / 100;
}

add(other: Money): Money {
return new Money(this.cents + other.cents);
}

subtract(other: Money): Money {
const result = this.cents - other.cents;
if (result < 0) {
throw new Error(Money invariant violated: negative result ${result});
}
return new Money(result);
}

multiply(factor: number): Money {
return new Money(Math.round(this.cents * factor));
}

divide(divisor: number): Money {
if (divisor === 0) throw new Error('Division by zero');
return new Money(Math.round(this.cents / divisor));
}

format(): string {
return $${(this.cents / 100).toFixed(2)};
}
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Portfolio Manager
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

export class PortfolioManager {
private portfolio: Portfolio;
private orderCounter = 0;
private tradeCounter = 0;
private onUpdate?: (portfolio: Portfolio) => void;

constructor(initialCash: number = 10000000, onUpdate?: (portfolio: Portfolio) => void) {
// initialCash in cents ($100,000.00 default)
this.portfolio = {
cash: initialCash,
positions: [],
trades: [],
totalValue: initialCash,
dayPnl: 0,
totalPnl: 0,
};
this.onUpdate = onUpdate;
}

getPortfolio(): Portfolio {
return { ...this.portfolio };
}

getPosition(symbol: string): Position | undefined {
return this.portfolio.positions.find(p => p.symbol === symbol);
}

/**

Execute order with secure verification binding.
Routes through secureExecute() wrapper for proof generation.
*/
async executeOrder(order: Order): Promise {
// Validate
if (order.quantity <= 0) {
throw new Error('Order quantity must be positive');
}
if (order.type === 'limit' && order.price <= 0) {
throw new Error('Limit order requires positive price');
}
const executionPrice = order.type === 'market' 
  ? await this.getMarketPrice(order.symbol)
  : order.price;

const total = order.quantity * executionPrice;

// Check invariants
if (order.side === 'buy') {
  if (total > this.portfolio.cash) {
    throw new Error(`Insufficient funds: need ${new Money(total).format()}, have ${new Money(this.portfolio.cash).format()}`);
  }
} else {
  const pos = this.getPosition(order.symbol);
  if (!pos || pos.quantity < order.quantity) {
    throw new Error(`Insufficient shares: have ${pos?.quantity || 0}, need ${order.quantity}`);
  }
}

// Build canonical trade payload for verification
const tradePayload = {
  version: '1.0',
  orderId: order.id,
  symbol: order.symbol,
  side: order.side,
  quantity: order.quantity,
  price: executionPrice,
  total,
  timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
};

// Generate proof via secureExecute() pattern
const proof = await this.secureExecute(tradePayload);

// Execute trade
const trade: Trade = {
  id: `T-${++this.tradeCounter}`,
  orderId: order.id,
  symbol: order.symbol,
  side: order.side,
  quantity: order.quantity,
  price: executionPrice,
  total,
  timestamp: tradePayload.timestamp,
  proof,
};

// Update portfolio state
this.applyTrade(trade);

// Notify
if (this.onUpdate) {
  this.onUpdate(this.getPortfolio());
}

return trade;
}

/**

secureExecute() — verification wrapper
Generates cryptographic proof of trade execution.
*/
private async secureExecute(payload: Record<string, unknown>): Promise {
const hash = await canonicalHash(payload);
// In production, this would use the identity private key
// For simulation, we generate a deterministic mock signature
const mockSignature = await this.mockSign(hash);

return {
  hash,
  signature: mockSignature,
  publicKey: 'mock-public-key-for-simulation',
  timestamp: payload.timestamp as string,
  algorithm: 'Ed25519-SHA256',
};
}

private async mockSign(hash: string): Promise {
// Deterministic mock signature for simulation
// In production: use tweetnacl.sign.detached(message, secretKey)
const encoder = new TextEncoder();
const data = encoder.encode(hash + 'trade-salt');
const hashBuffer = await crypto.subtle.digest('SHA-256', data);
return Array.from(new Uint8Array(hashBuffer))
.map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0'))
.join('');
}

private async getMarketPrice(symbol: string): Promise {
// Mock market price — in production, fetch from marketData.ts
let hash = 0;
for (let i = 0; i < symbol.length; i++) {
hash = ((hash << 5) - hash) + symbol.charCodeAt(i);
hash |= 0;
}
return 5000 + Math.abs(hash % 45000);
}

private applyTrade(trade: Trade) {
if (trade.side === 'buy') {
this.portfolio.cash -= trade.total;

  const existing = this.getPosition(trade.symbol);
  if (existing) {
    // Update average cost
    const totalCost = (existing.quantity * existing.avgCost) + trade.total;
    existing.quantity += trade.quantity;
    existing.avgCost = Math.round(totalCost / existing.quantity);
    existing.currentPrice = trade.price;
  } else {
    this.portfolio.positions.push({
      symbol: trade.symbol,
      quantity: trade.quantity,
      avgCost: trade.price,
      currentPrice: trade.price,
    });
  }
} else {
  // Sell
  this.portfolio.cash += trade.total;
  
  const existing = this.getPosition(trade.symbol);
  if (!existing) {
    throw new Error(`Cannot sell ${trade.symbol}: no position`);
  }
  
  if (existing.quantity === trade.quantity) {
    // Close position
    this.portfolio.positions = this.portfolio.positions.filter(p => p.symbol !== trade.symbol);
  } else {
    existing.quantity -= trade.quantity;
    existing.currentPrice = trade.price;
  }
}

this.portfolio.trades.push(trade);
this.recalculateValues();
}

private recalculateValues() {
const positionValue = this.portfolio.positions.reduce(
(sum, pos) => sum + (pos.quantity * pos.currentPrice),
0
);
this.portfolio.totalValue = this.portfolio.cash + positionValue;

// P&L calculation
const costBasis = this.portfolio.trades
  .filter(t => t.side === 'buy')
  .reduce((sum, t) => sum + t.total, 0);
const proceeds = this.portfolio.trades
  .filter(t => t.side === 'sell')
  .reduce((sum, t) => sum + t.total, 0);
const currentValue = positionValue;

this.portfolio.totalPnl = proceeds + currentValue - costBasis;
}

updatePrices(quotes: { symbol: string; price: number }[]) {
for (const quote of quotes) {
const pos = this.getPosition(quote.symbol);
if (pos) {
pos.currentPrice = quote.price;
}
}
this.recalculateValues();
if (this.onUpdate) {
this.onUpdate(this.getPortfolio());
}
}

generateOrderId(): string {
return O-${++this.orderCounter}-${Date.now()};
}
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Portfolio valuation utilities
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

export function calculatePositionPnl(position: Position): number {
return (position.currentPrice - position.avgCost) * position.quantity;
}

export function calculatePositionPnlPercent(position: Position): number {
if (position.avgCost === 0) return 0;
return Number(((position.currentPrice - position.avgCost) / position.avgCost * 100).toFixed(2));
}

export function formatCurrency(cents: number): string {
return $${(cents / 100).toFixed(2)};
}

export function formatPercent(value: number): string {
const sign = value >= 0 ? '+' : '';
return ${sign}${value.toFixed(2)}%;
}
'''

print(f"portfolio.ts: {len(portfolio_ts)} bytes")

PHASE 2 (continued): React Trading UI Components
============================================================

order_form_tsx = '''/**

OrderForm.tsx — Buy/sell order entry with validation
*/
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { Order } from '../../lib/portfolio';

interface OrderFormProps {
symbols: string[];
onSubmit: (order: Omit<Order, 'id' | 'status' | 'timestamp'>) => void;
portfolioCash: number;
positions: { symbol: string; quantity: number }[];
}

export const OrderForm: React.FC = ({ symbols, onSubmit, portfolioCash, positions }) => {
const [side, setSide] = useState<'buy' | 'sell'>('buy');
const [symbol, setSymbol] = useState(symbols[0] || '');
const [quantity, setQuantity] = useState('');
const [price, setPrice] = useState('');
const [type, setType] = useState<'market' | 'limit'>('market');
const [error, setError] = useState('');

const position = positions.find(p => p.symbol === symbol);
const maxSell = position?.quantity || 0;

const validate = (): boolean => {
setError('');

const qty = parseInt(quantity, 10);
if (!qty || qty <= 0) {
  setError('Quantity must be a positive integer');
  return false;
}

if (side === 'buy') {
  const estimatedCost = type === 'market' ? qty * 15000 : qty * parseInt(price || '0', 10);
  if (estimatedCost > portfolioCash) {
    setError(`Insufficient funds. Max: ${(portfolioCash / 100).toFixed(2)}`);
    return false;
  }
} else {
  if (qty > maxSell) {
    setError(`Max sell: ${maxSell} shares`);
    return false;
  }
}

if (type === 'limit' && (!price || parseInt(price, 10) <= 0)) {
  setError('Limit price required');
  return false;
}

return true;
};

const handleSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
e.preventDefault();
if (!validate()) return;

onSubmit({
  symbol,
  side,
  quantity: parseInt(quantity, 10),
  price: type === 'limit' ? parseInt(price, 10) : 0,
  type,
});

// Reset
setQuantity('');
setPrice('');
};

return (


Place Order
  <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
    {/* Side Toggle */}
    <div style={styles.sideToggle}>
      <button
        type="button"
        style={{...styles.sideBtn, ...(side === 'buy' ? styles.sideActiveBuy : {})}}
        onClick={() => setSide('buy')}
      >
        Buy
      </button>
      <button
        type="button"
        style={{...styles.sideBtn, ...(side === 'sell' ? styles.sideActiveSell : {})}}
        onClick={() => setSide('sell')}
      >
        Sell
      </button>
    </div>

    {/* Symbol */}
    <div style={styles.field}>
      <label style={styles.label}>Symbol</label>
      <select 
        style={styles.select} 
        value={symbol} 
        onChange={e => setSymbol(e.target.value)}
      >
        {symbols.map(s => (
          <option key={s} value={s}>{s}</option>
        ))}
      </select>
    </div>

    {/* Type */}
    <div style={styles.field}>
      <label style={styles.label}>Order Type</label>
      <div style={styles.typeToggle}>
        <button
          type="button"
          style={{...styles.typeBtn, ...(type === 'market' ? styles.typeActive : {})}}
          onClick={() => setType('market')}
        >
          Market
        </button>
        <button
          type="button"
          style={{...styles.typeBtn, ...(type === 'limit' ? styles.typeActive : {})}}
          onClick={() => setType('limit')}
        >
          Limit
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>

    {/* Quantity */}
    <div style={styles.field}>
      <label style={styles.label}>Quantity</label>
      <input
        type="number"
        style={styles.input}
        value={quantity}
        onChange={e => setQuantity(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="0"
        min="1"
      />
      {side === 'sell' && (
        <div style={styles.hint}>Max: {maxSell} shares</div>
      )}
    </div>

    {/* Price (limit only) */}
    {type === 'limit' && (
      <div style={styles.field}>
        <label style={styles.label}>Limit Price ($)</label>
        <input
          type="number"
          style={styles.input}
          value={price}
          onChange={e => setPrice(e.target.value)}
          placeholder="0.00"
          step="0.01"
          min="0.01"
        />
      </div>
    )}

    {error && (
      <div style={styles.error}>{error}</div>
    )}

    <button type="submit" style={styles.submitBtn}>
      {side === 'buy' ? 'Buy' : 'Sell'} {symbol}
    </button>
  </form>
</div>
);
};

const styles: Record<string, React.CSSProperties> = {

},

trade_history_tsx = '''/**

TradeHistory.tsx — Executed trades list with verification status
*/
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { Trade, formatCurrency } from '../../lib/portfolio';

interface TradeHistoryProps {
trades: Trade[];
}

export const TradeHistory: React.FC = ({ trades }) => {
const [expandedTrade, setExpandedTrade] = useState<string | null>(null);

const toggleExpand = (tradeId: string) => {
setExpandedTrade(expandedTrade === tradeId ? null : tradeId);
};

return (


Trade History
  {trades.length === 0 ? (
    <div style={styles.empty}>No trades executed</div>
  ) : (
    <div style={styles.tradeList}>
      {trades.slice().reverse().map(trade => (
        <TradeItem 
          key={trade.id} 
          trade={trade} 
          expanded={expandedTrade === trade.id}
          onToggle={() => toggleExpand(trade.id)}
        />
      ))}
    </div>
  )}
</div>
);
};

const TradeItem: React.FC<{
trade: Trade;
expanded: boolean;
onToggle: () => void;
}> = ({ trade, expanded, onToggle }) => {
const sideColor = trade.side === 'buy' ? '#00ff88' : '#ff3333';
const hasProof = !!trade.proof;

return (




<span style={{...styles.sideBadge, color: sideColor, borderColor: sideColor}}>
{trade.side.toUpperCase()}

{trade.symbol}
{trade.quantity} shares
@ {formatCurrency(trade.price)}
{formatCurrency(trade.total)}


{hasProof && (
✓ Verified
)}
{new Date(trade.timestamp).toLocaleTimeString()}
{expanded ? '▲' : '▼'}

  {expanded && trade.proof && (
    <div style={styles.proofDetails}>
      <h4 style={styles.proofHeader}>Verification Proof</h4>
      <div style={styles.proofRow}>
        <span style={styles.proofLabel}>Hash</span>
        <span style={styles.proofValue}>{trade.proof.hash}</span>
      </div>

        <span style={styles.proofLabel}>Timestamp</span>
        <span style={styles.proofValue}>{trade.proof.timestamp}</span>
      </div>
    </div>
  )}
</div>
);

price_chart_tsx = '''/**

PriceChart.tsx — Simple price visualization using SVG
Lightweight chart without external dependencies.
Shows price history as a line chart with gradient fill.
*/
import React, { useMemo } from 'react';

interface PricePoint {
timestamp: string;
price: number; // cents
}

interface PriceChartProps {
data: PricePoint[];
symbol: string;
width?: number;
height?: number;
}

export const PriceChart: React.FC = ({
data,
symbol,
width = 400,
height = 200
}) => {
const { path, fillPath, min, max, current } = useMemo(() => {
if (data.length < 2) return { path: '', fillPath: '', min: 0, max: 0, current: 0 };

const prices = data.map(d => d.price);
const min = Math.min(...prices);
const max = Math.max(...prices);
const range = max - min || 1;
const current = prices[prices.length - 1];

const padding = { top: 10, right: 10, bottom: 30, left: 50 };
const chartW = width - padding.left - padding.right;
const chartH = height - padding.top - padding.bottom;

const points = data.map((d, i) => {
  const x = padding.left + (i / (data.length - 1)) * chartW;
  const y = padding.top + chartH - ((d.price - min) / range) * chartH;
  return { x, y };
});

const linePath = points.reduce((path, p, i) => {
  return path + (i === 0 ? `M ${p.x} ${p.y}` : ` L ${p.x} ${p.y}`);
}, '');

const fill = linePath + 
  ` L ${points[points.length - 1].x} ${height - padding.bottom}` +
  ` L ${points[0].x} ${height - padding.bottom} Z`;

return { path: linePath, fillPath: fill, min, max, current };
}, [data, width, height]);

const change = data.length > 1
? ((current - data[0].price) / data[0].price * 100)
: 0;
const changeColor = change >= 0 ? '#00ff88' : '#ff3333';

return (



{symbol}
${(current / 100).toFixed(2)}
<span style={{...styles.change, color: changeColor}}>
{change >= 0 ? '+' : ''}{change.toFixed(2)}%

  <svg width={width} height={height} style={styles.svg}>
    <defs>
      <linearGradient id={`gradient-${symbol}`} x1="0" y1="0" x2="0" y2="1">
        <stop offset="0%" stopColor={change >= 0 ? '#00ff88' : '#ff3333'} stopOpacity="0.3" />
        <stop offset="100%" stopColor={change >= 0 ? '#00ff88' : '#ff3333'} stopOpacity="0" />
      </linearGradient>
    </defs>
    
    {/* Grid lines */}
    {[0, 0.25, 0.5, 0.75, 1].map(t => (
      <line
        key={t}
        x1={50}
        y1={10 + t * 160}
        x2={width - 10}
        y2={10 + t * 160}
        stroke="#1a1a1a"
        strokeWidth={1}
      />
    ))}
    
    {/* Y-axis labels */}
    {[0, 0.25, 0.5, 0.75, 1].map(t => {
      const price = min + (1 - t) * (max - min);
      return (
        <text
          key={t}
          x={45}
          y={15 + t * 160}
          fill="#555"
          fontSize="10"
          fontFamily="SF Mono, monospace"
          textAnchor="end"
        >
          ${(price / 100).toFixed(0)}
        </text>
      );
    })}
    
    {/* Fill area */}
    <path d={fillPath} fill={`url(#gradient-${symbol})`} />
    
    {/* Line */}
    <path 
      d={path} 
      fill="none" 
      stroke={change >= 0 ? '#00ff88' : '#ff3333'} 
      strokeWidth={2}
    />
    
    {/* Current price dot */}
    {data.length > 0 && (
      <circle
        cx={width - 60}
        cy={10 + 160 - ((current - min) / (max - min || 1)) * 160}
        r={4}
        fill={change >= 0 ? '#00ff88' : '#ff3333'}
      />
    )}
  </svg>
</div>
);
};

const styles: Record<string, React.CSSProperties> = {
container: {
background: '#111',
border: '1px solid #333',
borderRadius: '12px',
padding: '20px',
color: '#e0e0e0',
fontFamily: "'SF Pro Display', -apple-system, sans-serif",
},
header: {
display: 'flex',
alignItems: 'center',
gap: '12px',
marginBottom: '16px',
},
symbol: {
fontSize: '16px',
fontWeight: 700,
color: '#ff3333',
},
price: {
fontSize: '20px',
fontWeight: 700,
fontFamily: "'SF Mono', monospace",
},
change: {
fontSize: '13px',
fontWeight: 600,
fontFamily: "'SF Mono', monospace",
},
svg: {
display: 'block',
margin: '0 auto',
},
};
'''
